#7 3.455 Description:
#7 3.455 This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Update Note
#7 3.455 ===========
#7 3.455 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Reporting Issues
#7 3.455 ================
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
#7 3.455 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
#7 3.455 ====================================
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
#7 3.455 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
#7 3.455 - Note: Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Why some packages aren't built:
#7 3.455 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
#7 3.455 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Packages
#7 3.455 ========
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
#7 3.455 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Third-Party Python Modules
#7 3.455 ==========================
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
#7 3.455 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
#7 3.455 
#7 3.455 Sources
#7 3.455 =======
#7 3.455 The package sources are available at:
#7 3.455 https://github.com/deadsnakes/
#7 3.455
